First of all, the hotel is very new and clean, but the soundproofing of the room is very poor. The other rooms in the whole building are also like this. The pillows are very uncomfortable. People who want to sleep normally should not choose this hotel

Also, the shower water is too small and the water pressure is insufficient

The breakfast and service are very good, and the butler service attitude is also very good
